beginState: s32'CmnActJumpPre'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    attackEndDelay: 
    upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
      whiffCancelOptionBufferTime: s32'AirHover_6', 4
      whiffCancelOptionBufferTime: s32'AirHover_4', 4
      ifNot: Mem(IsLand)
        callSubroutine: s32'cmnLandingStiffadd'
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    checkLastStateName: s32'CmnActFDash'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      if: Mem(IsLand)
        addInertia: 12000
      endIf: 
    endIf: 
    checkLastStateName: s32'WildAssault'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      inertiaPercent: 90
    endIf: 
  endUpon: 
  gotoLabelIf: s32'FJumpPre', Mem(FJumpCheck)
  gotoLabelIf: s32'BJumpPre', Mem(BJumpCheck)
  sprite: s32'ino020_00', 4
  exitState: 
  beginLabel: s32'FJumpPre'
  sprite: s32'ino021_00', 4
  exitState: 
  beginLabel: s32'BJumpPre'
  sprite: s32'ino022_00', 4
endState:

beginState: s32'CmnActFDash'
  upon: (IMMEDIATE)
    setCommonActionMark: 1
    senkoInputNormal: 1
    bufferSpecialInput: 1
    enableRomanCancelMove: 1
    forceEnableBlueRomanCancel: 1
    upon: (IDLING)
      addTensionValAtMoveBBS: 12
      if: Mem(ActReg0)
        checkInput: (INPUT_ANY_FORWARD)
        ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
          checkInput: (INPUT_HOLD_DASH)
          ifNot: Mem(Tmp)
            clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
            gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
          endIf: 
        endIf: 
        checkInput: (INPUT_ANY_BACK)
        if: Mem(Tmp)
          clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
          gotoLabelRequests: s32'end'
        endIf: 
      endIf: 
    endUpon: 
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmnFDash', Val(2), Val(0), Val(0), Val(0)
    enableProximityBlock: 0
    enableBlock: 0
    enableBackDash: 0
    checkCurrentStateEntryName: s32'Cancel_FDash'
    if: Mem(Tmp)
      storeValue: Mem(ActReg1), Val(1)
      physicsXImpulse: 0, 0
    endIf: 
    else: 
      enableJump: 1
      enableBurst: 1
    endElse: 
    upon: (BEFORE_EXIT)
      velocityXPercent: 33
      resetGravity: 
    endUpon: 
  endUpon: 
  sprite: s32'ino032_01', 3
  sprite: s32'ino032_04', 3
  sprite: s32'ino032_05', 3
  velocityXRate: 115
  privateBankSfx: 1, s32'SE_BTL_INO_01', 70
  physicsXImpulse: 0, 18000
  physicsYImpulse: 0, 7500
  setGravity: 0
  enableJump: 0
  upon: (AFTER_EXIT)
    addInertia: 5000
  endUpon: 
  createObject: s32'Ino_Dash_Smoke01', (PLAYER_LAND)
  sprite: s32'ino032_06', 3
  physicsXImpulse: 0, 22000
  physicsYImpulse: 0, 7000
  ifNot: Mem(ActReg1)
    enableNormals: 1
    enableSpecials: 1
    enableAirBackDash: 1
    enableAirForwardDash: 1
    enableDoubleJump: 1
    enableProximityBlock: 1
    enableBlock: 1
  endIf: 
  sprite: s32'ino032_07', 3
  physicsXImpulse: 0, 26000
  physicsYImpulse: 0, 6500
  createObject: s32'Ino_Dash_Smoke02', (PLAYER_LAND)
  storeValue: Mem(ActReg0), Val(1)
  sprite: s32'ino032_05', 3
  physicsXImpulse: 0, 30000
  physicsYImpulse: 0, 6000
  sprite: s32'ino032_06', 3
  createObject: s32'Ino_Dash_Smoke03', (PLAYER_LAND)
  sprite: s32'ino032_07', 3
  sprite: s32'ino032_05', 3
  sprite: s32'ino032_06', 3
  sprite: s32'ino032_07', 3
  sprite: s32'ino032_05', 3
  endLabel: 
  beginLabel: s32'end'
  sprite: s32'ino032_08', 3
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (IDLING)
  clearRegisteredUponCode: (BEFORE_EXIT)
  velocityXPercent: 33
  resetGravity: 
  callSubroutine: s32'cmnNandemoCancelA'
  autoInputDirectionSearch: 0
  stopBankSfx: 0, 1
  sprite: s32'ino032_09', 3

endState:

  ifNot: Mem(ActReg0)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_AtkLv2', Val(3), Val(3), Val(0), Val(0)
    damage: Val(10)
    groundHitEffect: (AIR_FACE_UP)
    shortHitstop: 1
    hitRedRomanCancelTime: 4
    attackFrontDirection: (SELF)
    groundHitEffect: (AIR_FACE_UP)
    hitAirPushbackX: Val(17000)
    hitAirPushbackY: Val(20000)
    attackRange: 300000, 0, -1, -1

    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg12), Val(5)

    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg1), Val(100000)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg2), Val(0)
    ifOperation: (IS_GREATER_OR_EQUAL), Mem(ActReg1), Val(3)
      damage: Val(20)
      hitAirPushbackX: Val(10000)
      hitAirPushbackY: Val(45000)
      shortHitstop: 0
      attackEndDelay:

      hitAirPushbackYOverTime: Val(60), Val(10), Val(16)
      hitGravity: Val(0)
      hitGravityOverTime: Val(200), Val(6), Val(21)
      addGatlingOption: s32'KyougenD_Hasei'
    endIf: 
  endIf: 
  else: 
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_AtkLv4', Val(5), Val(5), Val(0), Val(0)
    damage: Val(10)
    groundHitEffect: (AIR_FACE_UP)
    shortHitstop: 1

    groundHitEffect: (AIR_FACE_UP)

    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaReg13), Val(5)
    callSubroutineWithArgs: s32'cmn_hosei', Val(1), Val(1), Val(0), Val(0)
    wallBlowoffType: (BLOWOFF_SLIDE)
    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg0), Val(-300000)

    storeValue: Mem(CmnCharaActReg2), Val(0)
